### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Show CollectiveKnowledge relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in (r.get('from_name','') + r.get('to_name','') + r.get('from','') + r.get('to',''))]\nprint(f'CollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint()\nprint(f'Total relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Check CollectiveKnowledge relations"
}
```

**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Show CollectiveKnowledge relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in (r.get('from_name','') + r.get('to_name','') + r.get('from','') + r.get('to',''))]\nprint(f'CollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint()\nprint(f'Total relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Check CollectiveKnowledge relations"
}
```

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Check for dupes\nfrom collections import Counter\nkeys = Counter()\nfor r in rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    k = f'{fr}__{rt}__{to}'\n    keys[k] += 1\ndupes = {k:v for k,v in keys.items() if v > 1}\nif dupes:\n    print('Duplicates:')\n    for k,v in dupes.items(): print(f'  {k}: {v}x')\nelse:\n    print('No duplicate relations')\n\n# Show CK relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in str(r)]\nprint(f'\\nCollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint(f'\\nTotal relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Verify relations after cleanup"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
No duplicate relations

CollectiveKnowledge relations (1):
  CollectiveKnowledge --[includes]--> Coding

Total relations: 49
```

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Check for dupes\nfrom collections import Counter\nkeys = Counter()\nfor r in rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    k = f'{fr}__{rt}__{to}'\n    keys[k] += 1\ndupes = {k:v for k,v in keys.items() if v > 1}\nif dupes:\n    print('Duplicates:')\n    for k,v in dupes.items(): print(f'  {k}: {v}x')\nelse:\n    print('No duplicate relations')\n\n# Show CK relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in str(r)]\nprint(f'\\nCollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint(f'\\nTotal relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Verify relations after cleanup"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
No duplicate relations

CollectiveKnowledge relations (1):
  CollectiveKnowledge --[includes]--> Coding

Total relations: 49
```

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Check for dupes\nfrom collections import Counter\nkeys = Counter()\nfor r in rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    k = f'{fr}__{rt}__{to}'\n    keys[k] += 1\ndupes = {k:v for k,v in keys.items() if v > 1}\nif dupes:\n    print('Duplicates:')\n    for k,v in dupes.items(): print(f'  {k}: {v}x')\nelse:\n    print('No duplicate relations')\n\n# Show CK relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in str(r)]\nprint(f'\\nCollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint(f'\\nTotal relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Verify relations after cleanup"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
No duplicate relations

CollectiveKnowledge relations (1):
  CollectiveKnowledge --[includes]--> Coding

Total relations: 49
```

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Check for dupes\nfrom collections import Counter\nkeys = Counter()\nfor r in rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    k = f'{fr}__{rt}__{to}'\n    keys[k] += 1\ndupes = {k:v for k,v in keys.items() if v > 1}\nif dupes:\n    print('Duplicates:')\n    for k,v in dupes.items(): print(f'  {k}: {v}x')\nelse:\n    print('No duplicate relations')\n\n# Show CK relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in str(r)]\nprint(f'\\nCollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint(f'\\nTotal relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Verify relations after cleanup"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
No duplicate relations

CollectiveKnowledge relations (1):
  CollectiveKnowledge --[includes]--> Coding

Total relations: 49
```

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "curl -s 'http://localhost:8080/api/relations?team=coding' | python3 -c \"\nimport sys, json\ndata = json.load(sys.stdin)\nrels = data if isinstance(data, list) else data.get('relations', [])\n# Check for dupes\nfrom collections import Counter\nkeys = Counter()\nfor r in rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    k = f'{fr}__{rt}__{to}'\n    keys[k] += 1\ndupes = {k:v for k,v in keys.items() if v > 1}\nif dupes:\n    print('Duplicates:')\n    for k,v in dupes.items(): print(f'  {k}: {v}x')\nelse:\n    print('No duplicate relations')\n\n# Show CK relations\nck_rels = [r for r in rels if 'CollectiveKnowledge' in str(r)]\nprint(f'\\nCollectiveKnowledge relations ({len(ck_rels)}):')\nfor r in ck_rels:\n    fr = r.get('from_name') or r.get('from','')\n    to = r.get('to_name') or r.get('to','')\n    rt = r.get('relation_type') or r.get('relationType','')\n    print(f'  {fr} --[{rt}]--> {to}')\nprint(f'\\nTotal relations: {len(rels)}')\n\"",
  "description": "Verify relations after cleanup"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
No duplicate relations

CollectiveKnowledge relations (1):
  CollectiveKnowledge --[includes]--> Coding

Total relations: 49
```

  "description": "Find orphaned insight files properly"
}

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:00:12 UTC [07:00:12 CEST]

**System Action:** (Initiated automatically)

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "python3 -c \"\nimport subprocess, json, os\n\nresult = subprocess.run(['curl', '-s', 'http://localhost:8080/api/entities?team=coding&limit=50'], capture_output=True, text=True)\ndata = json.loads(result.stdout)\nentities = data.get('entities', data) if isinstance(data, dict) else data\nremaining = {e['entity_name'] for e in entities}\n\ninsights_dir = 'knowledge-management/insights'\ndeleted = 0\nfor f in os.listdir(insights_dir):\n    if f.endswith('.md'):\n        name = f[:-3]\n        if name not in remaining and name != 'Usage':\n            os.remove(os.path.join(insights_dir, f))\n            deleted += 1\nprint(f'Deleted {deleted} orphaned insight files')\nprint(f'Remaining: {len(os.listdir(insights_dir))} files')\n\"",
  "description": "Delete orphaned insight files"
}
```

Skip garbage\n        if is_garbage(content):\n            continue\n        \n        # Skip verbose LLM paragraphs\n        if is_verbose_llm_paragraph(content):\n            continue\n        \n        # Dedup by first 100 chars\n        key = content[:100].strip()\n        if key in seen:\n            continue\n        seen.add(key)\n        \n        new_obs.append(o)\n    \n    if len(new_obs) != len(obs):\n        # Update via PUT API\n        update = {'observations': new_obs}\n        req = urllib.request.Request(\n            f'{VKB}/api/entities/{name}?team=coding',\n            data=json.dumps(update).encode(),\n            headers={'Content-Type': 'application/json'},\n            method='PUT'\n        )\n        try:\n            with urllib.request.urlopen(req) as resp:\n                result = json.loads(resp.read())\n            print(f'{name}: {len(obs)} -> {len(new_obs)} observations (removed {len(obs)-len(new_obs)})')\n            cleaned += 1\n        except Exception as ex:\n            print(f'{name}: ERROR - {ex}')\n\nprint(f'\\nCleaned {cleaned} entities')\nPYEOF",

process.env.VKB_URL || 'http://localhost:8080';\nconst args = process.argv.slice(2);\nconst DRY_RUN = args.includes('--dry-run');\nconst TEAM = (args.find(a => a.startsWith('--team=')) || '--team=coding').split('=')[1];\n\n// ─── Load manifest ───\nconst manifestPath = join(__dirname, '..', 'integrations', 'mcp-server-semantic-analysis', 'config', 'component-manifest.yaml');\nconst manifest = parse(readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));\n\n// ─── API helpers ───\nasync function apiGet(path) {\n  const res = await fetch(`${VKB}${path}`);\n  return res.json();\n}\n\nasync function apiPost(path, body) {\n  const res = await fetch(`${VKB}${path}`, {\n    method: 'POST',\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify(body)\n  });\n  return res.json();\n}\n\nasync function apiPut(path, body) {\n  const res = await fetch(`${VKB}${path}`, {\n    method: 'PUT',\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    body: JSON.stringify(body)\n  });\n  return res.json();\n}\n\nasync function apiDelete(path) {\n  const res = await fetch(`${VKB}${path}`, { method: 'DELETE' });\n  return res.json();\n}\n\n// ─── Build classification rules from manifest ───\nfunction buildClassifier(manifest) {\n  const rules = [];\n  for (const comp of manifest.components) {\n    // L2 children first (more specific match wins)\n    if (comp.children) {\n      for (const child of comp.children) {\n        rules.push({\n          name: child.name,\n          parent: comp.name,\n          level: 2,\n          keywords: child.keywords || [],\n          aliases: child.aliases || [],\n          description: child.description\n        });\n      }\n    }\n    rules.push({\n      name: comp.name,\n      parent: manifest.project.name,\n      level: 1,\n      keywords: comp.keywords || [],\n      aliases: comp.aliases || [],\n      description: comp.description\n    });\n  }\n  return rules;\n}\n\nfunction classifyEntity(entityName, observations, rules) {\n  const text = [\n    entityName,\n    ...(observations || []).map(o => typeof o === 'string' ? o : o.content || '')\n  ].join(' ').toLowerCase();\n\n  let bestMatch = null;\n  let bestScore = 0;\n\n  // Check L2 rules first, then L1\n  for (const rule of rules) {\n    let score = 0;\n    for (const kw of rule.keywords) {\n      if (text.includes(kw.toLowerCase())) score += 1;\n    }\n    for (const alias of rule.aliases) {\n      if (text.includes(alias.toLowerCase())) score += 2;\n    }\n    // Name substring match\n    if (entityName.toLowerCase().includes(rule.name.toLowerCase())) score += 5;\n\n    if (score > bestScore) {\n      bestScore = score;\n      bestMatch = rule;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Fallback to CodingPatterns\n  if (!bestMatch || bestScore < 1) {\n    bestMatch = rules.find(r => r.name === 'CodingPatterns');\n  }\n  return bestMatch;\n}\n\n// ─── Main ───\nasync function main() {\n  console.log(`\\n=== Hierarchy Migration ${DRY_RUN ? '(DRY RUN)' : ''} ===\\n`);\n\n  const rules = buildClassifier(manifest);\n  console.log(`Loaded ${rules.length} classification rules from manifest\\n`);\n\n  // Fetch existing entities\n  const data = await apiGet(`/api/entities?team=${TEAM}&limit=500`);\n  const entities = data.entities || data;\n  console.log(`Found ${entities.length} existing entities\\n`);\n\n  // Existing entity names\n  const existingNames = new Set(entities.map(e => e.entity_name));\n\n  // ─── Step 1: Create scaffold nodes ───\n  console.log('── Step 1: Create scaffold nodes ──\\n');\n\n  const scaffoldNodes = [];\n  for (const comp of manifest.components) {\n    scaffoldNodes.push({\n      name: comp.name,\n      level: 1,\n      parent: manifest.project.name,\n      description: comp.description,\n      children: (comp.children || []).map(c => c.name)\n    });\n    if (comp.children) {\n      for (const child of comp.children) {\n        scaffoldNodes.push({\n          name: child.name,\n          level: 2,\n          parent: comp.name,\n          description: child.description,\n          children: []\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  for (const node of scaffoldNodes) {\n    const action = existingNames.has(node.name) ? 'UPDATE' : 'CREATE';\n    console.log(`  ${action} L${node.level} ${node.name} (parent: ${node.parent})`);\n\n    if (!DRY_RUN) {\n      const body = {\n        name: node.name,\n        entityType: node.level === 1 ? 'Component' : 'SubComponent',\n        observations: [node.description],\n        significance: 8,\n        team: TEAM,\n        parentEntityName: node.parent,\n        hierarchyLevel: node.level,\n        isScaffoldNode: true,\n        childEntityNames: node.children\n      };\n\n      if (action === 'CREATE') {\n        await apiPost('/api/entities', body);\n      } else {\n        await apiPut(`/api/entities/${encodeURIComponent(node.name)}?team=${TEAM}`, body);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Also update the Coding project node\n  console.log(`  UPDATE L0 ${manifest.project.name} (root)`);\n  if (!DRY_RUN) {\n    const codingEntity = entities.find(e => e.entity_name === 'Coding');\n    await apiPut(`/api/entities/Coding?team=${TEAM}`, {\n      entityType: 'Project',\n      observations: codingEntity?.observations || [manifest.project.description],\n      significance: 10,\n      team: TEAM,\n      parentEntityName: 'CollectiveKnowledge',\n      hierarchyLevel: 0,\n      isScaffoldNode: true,\n      childEntityNames: manifest.components.map(c => c.name)\n    });\n  }\n\n  console.log(`\\n  Created/updated ${scaffoldNodes.length + 1} scaffold nodes\\n`);\n\n  // ─── Step 2: Classify existing leaf entities ───\n  console.log('── Step 2: Classify leaf entities ──\\n');\n\n  const classifications = {};\n  const scaffoldNames = new Set(scaffoldNodes.map(n => n.name));\n  scaffoldNames.add('Coding');\n  scaffoldNames.add('CollectiveKnowledge');\n\n  for (const entity of entities) {\n    const name = entity.entity_name;\n    if (scaffoldNames.has(name)) continue; // Skip scaffold/system nodes\n\n    const match = classifyEntity(name, entity.observations, rules);\n    if (match) {\n      classifications[name] = match;\n      console.log(`  ${name} → ${match.name} (L${match.level})`);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // ─── Step 3: Apply hierarchy to classified entities ───\n  console.log('\\n── Step 3: Apply hierarchy fields ──\\n');\n\n  for (const [entityName, match] of Object.entries(classifications)) {\n    const entity = entities.find(e => e.entity_name === entityName);\n    if (!entity) continue;\n\n    console.log(`  ${entityName}: parentEntityName=${match.name}, hierarchyLevel=${match.level + 1}`);\n\n    if (!DRY_RUN) {\n      await apiPut(`/api/entities/${encodeURIComponent(entityName)}?team=${TEAM}`, {\n        entityType: entity.entity_type,\n        observations: entity.observations,\n        team: TEAM,\n        parentEntityName: match.name,\n        hierarchyLevel: match.level + 1, // Children are one level below their parent\n        isScaffoldNode: false,\n        childEntityNames: []\n      });\n    }\n  }\n\n  // ─── Step 4: Rewire relations ───\n  console.log('\\n── Step 4: Rewire relations ──\\n');\n\n  // Delete old flat Coding→entity contains edges\n  const relData = await apiGet(`/api/relations?team=${TEAM}`);\n  const relations = relData.relations || relData;\n  const flatContains = relations.filter(r =>\n    (r.from_name === 'Coding' || r.from === 'Coding') &&\n    (r.relation_type === 'contains' || r.relationType === 'contains')\n  );\n  console.log(`  Found ${flatContains.length} flat Coding→entity 'contains' edges to rewire`);\n\n  for (const rel of flatContains) {\n    const target = rel.to_name || rel.to;\n    const match = classifications[target];\n    if (!match) continue; // scaffold nodes keep their direct link\n\n    if (!DRY_RUN) {\n      // Delete old flat edge\n      await apiDelete(`/api/relations?from=Coding&to=${encodeURIComponent(target)}&team=${TEAM}&type=contains`);\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Create new hierarchical contains edges (parent → child)\n  const parentChildren = {};\n  for (const [entityName, match] of Object.entries(classifications)) {\n    if (!parentChildren[match.name]) parentChildren[match.name] = [];\n    parentChildren[match.name].push(entityName);\n  }\n\n  // Also scaffold→scaffold edges\n  for (const node of scaffoldNodes) {\n    for (const childName of node.children) {\n      if (!parentChildren[node.name]) parentChildren[node.name] = [];\n      if (!parentChildren[node.name].includes(childName)) {\n        parentChildren[node.name].push(childName);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Coding → L1 contains edges\n  for (const comp of manifest.components) {\n    if (!parentChildren[manifest.project.name]) parentChildren[manifest.project.name] = [];\n    if (!parentChildren[manifest.project.name].includes(comp.name)) {\n      parentChildren[manifest.project.name].push(comp.name);\n    }\n  }\n\n  let edgesCreated = 0;\n  for (const [parent, children] of Object.entries(parentChildren)) {\n    for (const child of children) {\n      console.log(`  ${parent} → contains → ${child}`);\n      if (!DRY_RUN) {\n        await apiPost('/api/relations', {\n          from: parent,\n          to: child,\n          type: 'contains',\n          team: TEAM\n        });\n        edgesCreated++;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Update childEntityNames on scaffold nodes\n  if (!DRY_RUN) {\n    for (const node of scaffoldNodes) {\n      const allChildren = parentChildren[node.name] || [];\n      if (allChildren.length > 0) {\n        const entity = (await apiGet(`/api/entities?team=${TEAM}&limit=500`)).entities.find(e => e.entity_name === node.name);\n        if (entity) {\n          await apiPut(`/api/entities/${encodeURIComponent(node.name)}?team=${TEAM}`, {\n            entityType: entity.entity_type,\n            observations: entity.observations,\n            team: TEAM,\n            parentEntityName: node.parent,\n            hierarchyLevel: node.level,\n            isScaffoldNode: true,\n            childEntityNames: allChildren\n          });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  console.log(`\\n  Created ${edgesCreated} hierarchical 'contains' edges`);\n\n  // ─── Summary ───\n  console.log('\\n=== Migration Summary ===\\n');\n  console.log(`  Scaffold nodes: ${scaffoldNodes.length + 1}`);\n  console.log(`  Classified entities: ${Object.keys(classifications).length}`);\n  console.log(`  New contains edges: ${edgesCreated}`);\n  console.log(`  Mode: ${DRY_RUN ? 'DRY RUN (no changes made)' : 'LIVE'}`);\n  console.log('');\n}\n\nmain().catch(err => {\n  console.error('Migration failed:', err);\n  process.exit(1);\n});\n"
}

### Glob - 2026-03-04 06:59:08 UTC [07:59:08 CEST]

**User Request:** # Session Logs (/sl) - Session Continuity Command

Load and summarize recent Live Session Logs (LSL) to provide continuity from previous work sessions.

## Instructions

**Goal**: Load recent LSL files and produce a summary to establish context continuity.

### Step 1: Determine Current Project

1. Get the current working directory
2. Identify the project name (the directory name containing `.specstory/history`)
3. Note if this IS the `coding` project or a DIFFERENT project

### Step 2: Load LSL Files from Current Project

1. List files in `.specstory/history/` sorted by modification time (most recent first)
2. Load the **most recent** LSL file
3. Check file size/content length:
   - If file is **short** (less than 50KB or fewer than 500 lines of actual content), also load 1-2 previous files
   - "Short" means the session was brief and may not have enough context
4. Note the **timestamp range** from the oldest loaded file's filename (format: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM`)

### Step 3: Load Coding Project LSL Files (Cross-Project Context)

**Only if current project is NOT `coding`:**

1. Check `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/` for LSL files
2. Find files that fall within or overlap the timestamp range from Step 2
3. Load the most recent coding LSL file from that time range
4. If that file is short, also load 1-2 previous files from coding

**If current project IS `coding`:** Skip this step (already handled in Step 2)

### Step 4: Produce Summary

Create a concise summary covering:

1. **Time Range**: When these sessions occurred
2. **Projects Involved**: Which projects had activity
3. **Key Topics/Tasks**: Main things worked on in each session
4. **Current State**: What was left in progress or recently completed
5. **Suggested Next Steps**: Any obvious continuity items

Format the summary as:

```
## Session Continuity Summary

**Time Range**: [oldest file date] to [newest file date]
**Projects**: [list of projects with activity]

### Recent Work:
- [Project A]: [Brief description of main tasks]
- [Project B]: [Brief description of main tasks]

### Current State:
[What was in progress or just completed]

### Suggested Continuity:
[Any obvious next steps or items to pick up]
```

## File Selection Logic

- **Primary criterion**: Recency (most recent first)
- **Secondary criterion**: Length (short files trigger loading more files)
- **Tertiary criterion**: Cross-project relevance (coding project files during same timeframe)

## Size Thresholds

- **Short file**: < 50KB or < 500 lines → load additional files
- **Medium file**: 50KB-200KB → sufficient context alone
- **Large file**: > 200KB → definitely sufficient, may want to focus on recent sections

## Path Constants

- Current project LSL: `.specstory/history/`
- Coding project LSL: `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/`

## User Arguments

If user provides ``:
- Number (e.g., "3"): Load exactly that many recent files per project
- "all": Load all files from today
- Empty/default: Use automatic length-based detection

---

{
  "pattern": ".specstory/history/*.md"
}

### Step 4: Produce Summary

Create a concise summary covering:

1. **Time Range**: When these sessions occurred
2. **Projects Involved**: Which projects had activity
3. **Key Topics/Tasks**: Main things worked on in each session
4. **Current State**: What was left in progress or recently completed
5. **Suggested Next Steps**: Any obvious continuity items

Format the summary as:

```
## Session Continuity Summary

**Time Range**: [oldest file date] to [newest file date]
**Projects**: [list of projects with activity]

### Recent Work:
- [Project A]: [Brief description of main tasks]
- [Project B]: [Brief description of main tasks]

### Current State:
[What was in progress or just completed]

### Suggested Continuity:
[Any obvious next steps or items to pick up]
```

## File Selection Logic

- **Primary criterion**: Recency (most recent first)
- **Secondary criterion**: Length (short files trigger loading more files)
- **Tertiary criterion**: Cross-project relevance (coding project files during same timeframe)

## Size Thresholds

- **Short file**: < 50KB or < 500 lines → load additional files
- **Medium file**: 50KB-200KB → sufficient context alone
- **Large file**: > 200KB → definitely sufficient, may want to focus on recent sections

## Path Constants

- Current project LSL: `.specstory/history/`
- Coding project LSL: `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/`

## User Arguments

If user provides ``:
- Number (e.g., "3"): Load exactly that many recent files per project
- "all": Load all files from today
- Empty/default: Use automatic length-based detection

---

**Begin by identifying the current project and loading the most recent LSL file.**

**Tool:** Bash
**Input:** ```json
{
  "command": "ls -t /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/*.md | head -5",
  "description": "List 5 most recent session log files"
}
```

### Bash - 2026-03-04 06:59:08 UTC [07:59:08 CEST]

**User Request:** # Session Logs (/sl) - Session Continuity Command

Load and summarize recent Live Session Logs (LSL) to provide continuity from previous work sessions.

## Instructions

**Goal**: Load recent LSL files and produce a summary to establish context continuity.

### Step 1: Determine Current Project

1. Get the current working directory
2. Identify the project name (the directory name containing `.specstory/history`)
3. Note if this IS the `coding` project or a DIFFERENT project

### Step 2: Load LSL Files from Current Project

1. List files in `.specstory/history/` sorted by modification time (most recent first)
2. Load the **most recent** LSL file
3. Check file size/content length:
   - If file is **short** (less than 50KB or fewer than 500 lines of actual content), also load 1-2 previous files
   - "Short" means the session was brief and may not have enough context
4. Note the **timestamp range** from the oldest loaded file's filename (format: `YYYY-MM-DD_HHMM`)

### Step 3: Load Coding Project LSL Files (Cross-Project Context)

**Only if current project is NOT `coding`:**

1. Check `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/` for LSL files
2. Find files that fall within or overlap the timestamp range from Step 2
3. Load the most recent coding LSL file from that time range
4. If that file is short, also load 1-2 previous files from coding

**If current project IS `coding`:** Skip this step (already handled in Step 2)

### Step 4: Produce Summary

Create a concise summary covering:

1. **Time Range**: When these sessions occurred
2. **Projects Involved**: Which projects had activity
3. **Key Topics/Tasks**: Main things worked on in each session
4. **Current State**: What was left in progress or recently completed
5. **Suggested Next Steps**: Any obvious continuity items

Format the summary as:

```
## Session Continuity Summary

**Time Range**: [oldest file date] to [newest file date]
**Projects**: [list of projects with activity]

### Recent Work:
- [Project A]: [Brief description of main tasks]
- [Project B]: [Brief description of main tasks]

### Current State:
[What was in progress or just completed]

### Suggested Continuity:
[Any obvious next steps or items to pick up]
```

## File Selection Logic

- **Primary criterion**: Recency (most recent first)
- **Secondary criterion**: Length (short files trigger loading more files)
- **Tertiary criterion**: Cross-project relevance (coding project files during same timeframe)

## Size Thresholds

- **Short file**: < 50KB or < 500 lines → load additional files
- **Medium file**: 50KB-200KB → sufficient context alone
- **Large file**: > 200KB → definitely sufficient, may want to focus on recent sections

## Path Constants

- Current project LSL: `.specstory/history/`
- Coding project LSL: `/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.specstory/history/`

## User Arguments

If user provides ``:
- Number (e.g., "3"): Load exactly that many recent files per project
- "all": Load all files from today
- Empty/default: Use automatic length-based detection
